   ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'ntarikṣe viṣṇurvyakraṃsta traiṣṭubhena candasā tato	ca vayam dvizmaH antarikze vizNuH-vyakraMsta trEzwuBena candasA tatas-
   nirbhakto	nirBaktaH-
   yo 'smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ pṛthivyāṃ viṣṇurvyakraṃsta gāyatreṇa	yaH asmAn-dvezwi yam ca vayam dvizmaH pRTivyAm vizNuH-vyakraMsta gAyatreNa
   candasā	candasA
   tato nirbhakto yo 'smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'smādannādasyai	tatas nirBaktaH yaH asmAn-dvezwi yam ca vayam dvizmaH asmAt-annAdasyE
   pratiṣṭhāyā	pratizWAyA
   ityasyāṃ hīdaṃ sarvamannādyam pratiṣṭhita tasmādāhāsmādannādasyai	iti-asyAm hi-idam sarvam-annAdyam pratizWita tasmAt-Aha-asmAt-anna-AdasyE
   pratiṣṭhāyā	pratizWAyA
   iti	iti
   atha prāṅ prekṣate | prācī hi devānāṃ diktasmātprāṅ prekṣate	aTa prAF prekzate | prAcI hi devAnAm diS-tasmAt-prAF prekzate
   sa prekṣate | aganma svariti devā vai svaraganma devānityevaitadāha saṃ	sa prekzate | aganma svar-iti devAH vE svara-ganma devAn-iti-eva-etat-Aha saM
   jyotiṣābhūmeti saṃ devairabhūmetyevaitadāha	jyotizA-aBUma-iti sam devEH-aBUma-iti-eva-etat-Aha
   atha sūryamudīkṣate | saiṣā gatireṣāpratiṣṭhā tadetāṃ gatimetām pratiṣṭhāṃ	aTa sUryam-udIkzate | sA-ezA gatiH-ezA-pratizWA tat-etAm gatim-etAm pratizWAm
   gacati	gacati
   tasmātsūryamudīkṣate	tasmAt-sUryam-udIkzate
   sa udīkṣate | svayambhūrasi śreṣṭho raśmirityeṣa vai śreṣṭho	saH udIkzate | svayamBUH-asi SrezWaH raSmiH-iti-eza vE SrezWaH-
   raśmiryatsūryastasmādāha svayambhūrasi śreṣṭho raśmiriti varcodā asi varco	raSmiH-yat-sUryaH-tasmAt-Aha svayamBUH-asi SrezWaH raSmiH-iti varcA-udAH asi varcaH-
   me	me
   dehīti tvevāhaṃ bravīmīti ha smāha yājñavalkyastaddhyeva	dehi-iti tu-eva-aham bravImi-iti ha sma-Aha yAjQavalkyaH-tat-hi-eva
   brāhmaṇenaiṣṭhavyaṃ	brAhmaNena-ezWavyam
   yadbrahmavarcasī syādityuto ha smāhaupoditeya eṣa vāva mahyaṃ gā dāsyati	yat-brahmavarcasI syAt-iti-utaH ha sma-AhOpoditeyaH eza vAva mahyam gAH dAsyati
   godā	godA
   gā me dehītyevaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate so 'smai kāmaḥ samṛdhyate	gAH me dehi-iti-evam yam kAmam kAmayate saH asmE kAmaH samRDyate
   athāvartate | sūryasyāvṛtamanavāvarta iti tadetāṃ gatimetām pratiṣṭhāṃ	aTa-Avartate | sUryasya-AvRtam-anavAvartaH iti tat-etAm gatim-etAm pratizWAm
   gatvaitasyaivāvṛtamanvāvartate	gatvA-etasya-eva-AvRtam-anvAvartate
   atha gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhate | dvayaṃ tadyasmādgārhapatyamupatiṣṭhate gṛhā	aTa gArhapatyam-upatizWate | dvayam tat-yasmAt-gArhapatyam-upatizWate gRhA
   vai	vE
   gārhapatyo gṛhā vai pratiṣṭhā tadgṛheṣvevaitatpratiṣṭhāyām pratitiṣṭhati	gArhapatyaH gRhAH vE pratizWA tad-gRhezu-eva-etat-pratizWAyAm pratitizWati
   yāvadvevāsyeha mānuṣamāyustasmā evaitadupatiṣṭhate	yAvat-veva-asya-iha mAnuzam-AyuH-tasmE eva-etat-upatizWate
   tasmādgārhapatyamupatiṣṭhate	tasmAt-gArhapatyam-upatizWate
   sa upatiṣṭhate | agne gṛhapate sugṛhapatistvayāgne 'haṃ gṛhapatinā	saH upatizWate | agne gRhapate su-gRhapatiH-tvayA-agne aham gRhapatinA
   bhūyāsaṃ	BUyAsam
   sugṛhapatistvaṃ mayāgne gṛhapatinā bhūyā iti nātra tirohitamivāstyasthūri	su-gRhapatiH-tvam mayA-agne gRhapatinA BUyAH iti na-atra tirohitam-iva-asti-asTUri
   nau	nO
   gārhapatyāni santvityanārttāni nau gārhapatyāni santvityevaitadāha śataṃ	gArhapatyAni santu-iti-anArttAni nO gArhapatyAni santu-iti-eva-etat-Aha Satam
   himā iti	himA iti
   śataṃ varṣāṇi jīvyāsamityevaitadāha tadapyetadbruvannādriyetāpi hi	Satam varzANi jIvyAsam-iti-eva-etat-Aha tat-api-etat-bruvan=-Adriyeta-api hi
   bhūyāṃsi	BUyAMsi
   śatādvarṣebhyaḥ puruṣo jīvati tasmādapyetadbruvannādriyeta	SatAt-varzeByaH puruzaH jIvati tasmAt-api-etat-bruvan=-Adriyeta
   athāvartate | sūryasyāvṛtamanvāvarta iti tadetāṃ gatimetām pratiṣṭhāṃ	aTa-Avartate | sUryasya-AvRtam-anvAvartaH iti tat-etAm gatim-etAm pratizWAm
   gatvaitasyaivāvṛtamanvāvartate	gatvA-etasya-eva-AvRtam-anvAvartate
   atha putrasya nāma gṛhṇāti | idam me 'yaṃ vīryam putro 'nusaṃtanavaditi	aTa putrasya nAma gRhNAti | idam me ayam vIryam putraH anusaMtana-vat-iti
   yadi putro	yadi putraH-
   na syādapyātmana eva nāma gṛhṇīyāt	na syAt-api-AtmanaH eva nAma gRhNIyAt-
   athāhavanīyamupatiṣṭhate | prāṅne yajño 'nusaṃtiṣṭhātā iti	aTa-AhavanIyam-upatizWate | prAFne yajQaH anusaMtizWAtAH iti
   tūṣṇīmupatiṣṭhateatha	tUzNIm-upatizWata-iaTa
   vrataṃ visṛjate | idamahaṃ ya evāsmi so 'smītyamānuṣa iva vā etadbhavati	vratam visRjate | idam-aham yaH eva-asmi saH asmi-iti-amAnuzaH iva vE etat-Bavati
   yadvratamupaiti na hi tadavakalpate yadbrūyādidamahaṃ satyādanṛtamupaimīti	yat-vratam-upEti na hi tad-avakalpate yat-brUyAt-idam-aham satyAt-anRtam-upEmi-iti
   tadu	tat-u
   khalu punarmānuṣo bhavati tasmādidamahaṃ ya evāsmi sā 'smītyevaṃ vrataṃ	Kalu punar-mAnuzaH Bavati tasmAt-idam-aham yaH eva-asmi sA asmi-iti-evam vratam
   visṛjeta	visRjeta
